# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Move the left most nonzero
entry to the top ^K70ZXThu

Next pivot point
Is already now up
top after the 
first pivot point ^uBD0r6CS

Kill the entries below that
to create REF
(kill both above and bottom
entries for RREF) ^2hrdEPUQ

Ahaa! We have the REF! ^aD6eoz1J

To Get a RREF, first create a REF.

Then start with last pivot points, scale them into 1's and kill entries above them ^PNw4NBxv

Now kill ^Aewj8taQ

KILL! ^wRqXzbWU

Scale to 1 ^2658rGOn

AHAA! FINALLY! THE REDUCED ROW-ECHELON FORM ^VWWWsrUW
